```dockerfile
FROM ubuntu:22.04

ARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
ENV TZ=Europe/Berlin

# Install git separately first
RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y git

# Install other system dependencies
RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
    tzdata bash ca-certificates \
    curl sudo nano software-properties-common vim wget python3 python3-pip unzip tar apt-transport-https lsb-release \
    && ln -snf /usr/share/zoneinfo/$TZ /etc/localtime \
    && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*

WORKDIR /app

# Clone the repo
RUN git clone https://github.com/iris-sast/iris.git

WORKDIR /app/iris

# Install Miniconda
ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/bin:$PATH

RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
    chmod +x /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
    /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
    rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
    conda clean -afy

# Create the conda environment
RUN conda env create -f environment.yml

# Set up conda environment activation
SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
RUN echo "conda activate iris" >> ~/.bashrc

# CMD to run the tests will be configured later
CMD ["/bin/bash"]
```

```json
{
  "filename": "Dockerfile",
  "text": "FROM ubuntu:22.04\n\nARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive\nENV TZ=Europe/Berlin\n\n# Install git separately first\nRUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y git\n\n# Install other system dependencies\nRUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \\\n    tzdata bash ca-certificates \\\n    curl sudo nano software-properties-common vim wget python3 python3-pip unzip tar apt-transport-https lsb-release \\\n    && ln -snf /usr/share/zoneinfo/$TZ /etc/localtime \\\n    && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*\n\nWORKDIR /app\n\n# Clone the repo\nRUN git clone https://github.com/iris-sast/iris.git\n\nWORKDIR /app/iris\n\n# Install Miniconda for ARM\nENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda\nENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/bin:$PATH\n\nRUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-aarch64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \\\n    chmod +x /tmp/miniconda.sh && \\\n    /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \\\n    rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \\\n    conda clean -afy\n\n# Accept Terms of Service for conda channels\nRUN conda tos accept --override-channels --channel https://repo.anaconda.com/pkgs/main \\\n    && conda tos accept --override-channels --channel https://repo.anaconda.com/pkgs/r\n\n# Continue with conda environment setup from environment.yml\nRUN conda env create -f environment.yml\n\n# Set up conda environment activation\nSHELL [\"/bin/bash\", \"-c\"]\nRUN echo \"conda activate iris\" >> ~/.bashrc\n\n# CMD to run the tests will be configured later\nCMD [\"/bin/bash\"]"
```

6. How to run it robustly: I will change the Dockerfile content to reflect this choice. The amendment will specify a different Conda installer for a more compatible environment. The Dockerfile will look as follows:

```dockerfile
FROM ubuntu:22.04

ARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
ENV TZ=Europe/Berlin

RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y git

RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
    tzdata bash ca-certificates \
    curl sudo nano software-properties-common vim wget python3 python3-pip unzip tar apt-transport-https lsb-release \
    && ln -snf /usr/share/zoneinfo/$TZ /etc/localtime \
    && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*

WORKDIR /app

RUN git clone https://github.com/iris-sast/iris.git

WORKDIR /app/iris

ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/bin:$PATH

# Install Miniconda instead of Miniforge
RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
    chmod +x /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
    /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
    rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
    conda clean -afy

RUN conda tos accept --override-channels --channel https://repo.anaconda.com/pkgs/main \
    && conda tos accept --override-channels --channel https://repo.anaconda.com/pkgs/r

RUN conda env create -f environment.yml

SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
RUN echo "conda activate iris" >> ~/.bashrc

CMD ["/bin/bash"]
```

Here’s the Dockerfile content I plan to rewrite:

```dockerfile
FROM ubuntu:22.04

ARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
ENV TZ=Europe/Berlin

# Install git separately first
RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y git

# Install other system dependencies
RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
    tzdata bash ca-certificates \
    curl sudo nano software-properties-common vim wget python3 python3-pip unzip tar apt-transport-https lsb-release \
    && ln -snf /usr/share/zoneinfo/$TZ /etc/localtime \
    && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*

WORKDIR /app

# Clone the repository
RUN git clone https://github.com/iris-sast/iris.git
WORKDIR /app/iris

# Install Miniconda (verified link)
ENV CONDA_DIR=/opt/conda
ENV PATH=$CONDA_DIR/bin:$PATH

RUN wget --quiet https://repo.anaconda.com/miniconda/Miniconda3-latest-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
    chmod +x /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
    /tmp/miniconda.sh -b -p $CONDA_DIR && \
    rm /tmp/miniconda.sh && \
    conda clean -afy

# Accept the conda terms of service
RUN conda tos accept

# Create and activate the conda environment using environment.yml
RUN conda env create -f environment.yml

# Set up conda environment activation
SHELL ["/bin/bash", "-c"]
RUN echo "conda activate iris" >> ~/.bashrc

CMD ["/bin/bash"]
```

```dockerfile
# Activate the conda environment

# Specify command to keep the container running
CMD ["/bin/bash"]
```

6. **How to run it robustly**: I will write a Dockerfile tailored for this project. The Dockerfile will:
   - Use `python:3.10-slim` as the base image for a lightweight setup.
   - Install `git`, `curl`, and `wget` for repository access and downloads.
   - Download and install Miniforge as the Python package manager and setup the environment defined in `environment.yml`.

Here’s the exact content for the Dockerfile:
```dockerfile
FROM python:3.10-slim

# Set working directory
WORKDIR /app

# Install system dependencies and Miniforge
RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends git curl wget \
    && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/* \
    && wget --quiet https://github.com/conda-forge/miniforge/releases/latest/download/Miniforge3-Linux-x86_64.sh -O /tmp/miniforge.sh \
    && chmod +x /tmp/miniforge.sh \
    && /tmp/miniforge.sh -b -p /opt/conda \
    && rm /tmp/miniforge.sh

# Ensure conda is in PATH
ENV PATH="/opt/conda/bin:$PATH"

# Clone the repository
RUN git clone https://github.com/iris-sast/iris.git /app

# Download the environment.yml file
RUN wget https://raw.githubusercontent.com/iris-sast/iris/main/environment.yml

# Create the conda environment
RUN conda env create -f environment.yml

# Set command for the container
CMD ["/bin/bash"]
```
